The first method is to make three or four cauterisations in a line according to the length of the nose, following the shape of the liver cautery we mentioned earlier; do not press your hand on all the cauteries and have the patient lie prone on their back; another cautery method is to heat the double-nerve cautery as shown for shoulder dislocation, lift the heart upwards towards the nose where the patient's pain comes from the left side, and let the elevation by which you lifted the heart be according to the length of the body, with the cauteries being made in line with the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has gotten rid of pus over a long time, and this is better than the other treatments mentioned earlier.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for dropsy, except for the method called 'ascites'.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned before in divisions, and your treatment does not benefit the patient, then you must apply four cauterizations around the navel, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back on the spine, and one on the testicles; and let the cauterizations be close to the heart's apex.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After that, leave the open cauterization for a long time to get rid of pus, and do not leave the patient untreated after the cautery; healing would hasten, and the two intentions will come together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cautery for the belly shall be the bone we previously showed; and that for the back shall be olive-shaped, according to what was laid out before.
de l’enfleure des piez	The swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and they are full of yellow water, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger; lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, so as not to pierce the yellow water, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterwards make two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the small spade-shaped bone; let the cauteries be as long as this, one below the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg; leave the cauteries open for a long time without cleaning them, until the water comes out; then treat with the other treatments we have mentioned.
de la menoison	From the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When abdominal pain arises from cold and moisture, such that the retaining and digestive faculties which are in the stomach and intestine become weakened, and cannot be cured by ordinary remedies; and you see the patient suffer greatly with strong vitality, then make a large circular cautery on the stomach as described previously for the stomach cautery. Also four small subtle clavicle cauteries around the navel, two cauteries over the hips
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, apply a cautery to the wrist, one cautery on each elbow, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large [one], for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When hemorrhoids are found at the base of the spine, whether one or multiple, and they are old, consisting of large, cold, moist, corrupted humors, and treatment as described earlier is not effective, then apply cauterization: three cauterizations on the back's surface outside the lower spine in a triangular pattern, and one cauterization beneath the navel two fingers wide; if you suspect their stomach has cooled down and meat is not properly digested, and swelling of the face is observed, then apply one large cauterization to the stomach as mentioned earlier, another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all three cauterizations being clavicle-shaped; leave the cauterized areas open for a long period.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the site heal until it is completely healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is named "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat thethelul, heat the cautery as if it were a razor, then place it fully ignited on top of the treated thethelul; leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the surface of the wound, causing blood to flow out; do this once or twice, and if there is much thethelul, cauterize each area as we have described; after applying beneficial ointments treat them until they are healed; and if you use a large cautery on alchatim, it will be more effective.
de plaie mal curee	Of badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When a patient cannot bear the scalpel or incision, as we will describe in its place, such illness arises that can only be healed through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula develops and emits purulent matter along with foul-smelling moisture, you must first examine it carefully using an appropriate probe, taking care to know the entire length of the abscess.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizing iron like a razor, insert it into the fistula according to how far the probe went in, and repeat cauterization as needed until all the corrupt pus is burnt away, once or twice or three times depending on the extent of the damage; take care not to burn nerves or major veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and into the intestine, be aware of its location, do not make incisions where there is flesh, and remember it is not permanent; after treating the site until it heals, if the wound has been dry for a long time and the matter is removed, then know that the wound has healed completely; but if the matter is still present, know that the wound remains open, and the bone at its base is damaged; just as we will explain in one of our following teachings.
de la maladie des reins	En l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from cold comes to the loins, and there is severe windiness, and it does not take on a feminine nature, then you must perform cautery on the loins, one side and the other, with the clavicle cautery as we have said before; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauteries in a line, and they will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, such that the patient retains urine, then cauterize them on the outside part above the bladder, where the arm hairs begin, one on the right and one on the left, each cautery as long as a one-inch finger; perform an additional cautery on the back if needed, or two if necessary; make the cauteries clavicle according to the form previously described.
de la marris	From a marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow conception, and flowers are corrupted and their ends delay; and when they come, there is great pain: then it must be that we make three cauteries around the uterus, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries outside the back; and let the cautery be clamped, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hip.
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip socket, and due to this it moves from its place, and the signs are that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and you will find the location of the displacement visually, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip bone with a single cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the dislocation around the bone as it turns, so that the bone lies within the circle; and let this cautery be similar to that used for the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if these cauterizations are not available to you, then make three large olive-oil cauterizations, and let the cauterizations be as perfect as all hearts; treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the hip's pain.
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the socket of the hip, caused by cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said before but it is not working, and the illness is long-lasting: then you must purge the patient from thick foul humors with pills that stink, or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After performing the cauterization; and the method of cautery is twofold: namely, by means of burning medicines, or by fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Cautery with fire can be done in many ways, and one of them is as follows: apply three triangular cauteries on the hip bone like this; make them deep and large, leaving space between each one equal to the thickness of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped. Sometimes you cauterize in the middle over the head of the hip bone, so it becomes four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see fit, use the circular cautery we previously mentioned for hip dislocations; but make sure the circle encompasses the entire hip bone and all the flesh of the heart is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is the method employed for sciatica when pain is localized in the hip and does not extend to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	Et if it comes down to the thigh and leg, make two cauteries where the patient says the pain is located, and one above the ankle four fingers long on the left side somewhat less; let the cauterization be done with a lancet and burn away the thickness of the heart; and if the patient feels that the pain extends up to the toes or near them, then cauterize at three points where he feels the pain or cauterize with four points using what is called the "point" technique.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it is necessary, make more [cauteries]; and if you know that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then perform a cautery with either a lancet or circular technique; take great care in all your cauterizations to not leave the cautery for so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and cause even greater nuisance and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who underwent cauterization on the ankle of the foot, and they left it so that their leg became completely swollen, as well as their feet, and their feet were pierced and corrupted throughout.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After the abdominal operation which resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, cauterize both one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	The wise men said regarding cauterization of the hip, this is how it should be done: make such an iron tool that at its head is as big as a two-digit navel, or slightly less, and have it perforated with holes, spaced apart from each other by one thumb's width; these perforations should cover two parts, being also shaped like knots. There must be a well-crafted handle of iron attached to the tool; this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And be heated until it is all red and throw off sparks, then put it on top of the diseased hip joint and turn onto your sound side; cauterize once with one iron and leave for three days; afterwards make a plaster of butter, leaving the wound open long enough time; after healing by medicating until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says we use this cautery sparingly because of its appearance and also rarely see it being used; nevertheless it is one of the good cauteries which can be endured if not left on too long where it becomes painful.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The burning medical cautery is made from one instrument with interlacing bars, where the border of the door descends into it, and it can be made either from copper or iron on a long handle; its height being two spans and each section having the thickness of a finger's breadth; they are open underneath and above and join together in this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Afterwards, place the box of the hip on the patient lying on their sound side, and press your hand firmly onto the hip joint; then pour between the two circles a warm liquid that is heated by one-quarter fire, and let it remain for an hour's time, allowing the patient to endure its heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For if they find the cautery as painful as fire, and once this pain is past, raise your hand with an instrument and gently lift their hip in a warm bath, leaving it so for three days; then apply butter until that which was blackened by burning has been removed; let this remain three more days to draw out infection, and repeat the process of ointments until they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or down to the leg, make an instrument for him to hold according to what you have done at the hip similarly; and this is the method of the hot compress, which I have written about in the treatise on medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	where there is a small opening for liquid to flow out through which the point of a razor can enter; place over this pot another well-sealed pot, and put warm water and a cloth on top so that there are two fingers' worth above the powders when you have properly grasped it in your hand; leave it thus until warm water and vapor descend into the sealed pot, then take all this moisture and pour it back onto the chalk and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And so there will be much fever and it is administered in many medical practices and cauterizations of other members because it does similar work as fire, and has other medicines with which one can cauterize the hip well such as beeswax and acacia honey and hot soap; all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was cured of hip pain and sciatica, and he praises it greatly, saying that no other treatment was used, and he was healed immediately after this cure was performed, and he took a bath as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he says to do it in this way: take some fresh and dry verdigris, grind it finely with one pound of grease, apply it on the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is felt, bind it up; leave it for three hours or less depending on how much the patient feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let him enter the bath until his body is a little warmed up, and place him in bed, and the pain will disappear completely and he shall be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicines of cauterization without first evacuating the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's fat, it helps greatly; and the cautery should be done in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and cover it with old oil-based grease, and place it on the depression which is between the big toe and the one next to it, called the fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take dry goat's fat and hold it over the fire until it becomes charcoal, and place it on the linen, leaving it there until it is extinguished. Repeat this process again and do not cease doing so until you feel that it reaches up to the hip, and the pain has ceased; and such a manner of cauterization is called "goat's cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	From the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or due to impact or excessive loss, or because of similar spread matter that is cold, in none of these cases are caustic remedies good except for those caused by an influx of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	One must afterwards purge the patient with foul pills or other similar things that are applied to the back where the pain is felt, three lines marked out with ink, and in each line there should be five caustic remedies or more depending on their virtue and quantity that the patient can bear; and the caustic remedy ought to be performed like the cautery called "pin-prick"; but if you wish, do three or four using an intermediate sized chisel following this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	Many times this illness occurs in small children, and the signs of its onset are narrow shoulders when they rise up, and fear; you find in the lower back spine and in us the appearance that comes over other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this, and treat it, cauterize it with the cold cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery touches each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, cauterize around the spine with the sharp cautery using two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treat the place until it is healed according to what we have said, and be wary of applying cautery to a swollen area with nerve damage.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of joints is due to moisture that spreads to each member of the body, and when the pain comes in the foot, which the physician calls "gout" properly, and when it is caused by coldness and medicines cannot cure it, it is treated with cautery in this way: make a series of cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to act upon the front of the foot, make a single cauterization that we call a "dot.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains reach up to the knees and other joints, and this happens frequently, make three cauterizations on each knee or four on each side, all with the olive-shaped cautery; and if you need more, do more, but do not hold your hand there longer than it takes for the heartwood of the stake to burn.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cautery as we described in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make points around the wrist with two lines; and if there remains any pain in the fingers, make points on each joint and over the hair of the hand; and if the pains come down to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and provide good care for the patient and give them medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good care and remove the phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	On fracture of the hip joint.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When fracture occurs in the groin, and the bones descend towards the thighs and it is recent, you must make sure that on the day of cure he does not eat anything; and have him use things that empty his stomach so that the faeces descend from his belly; afterwards, make him sit on his back between your hands, command him to hold his breath until the bones are mended, and bring them together with your two hands, and cauterize below the fracture onto the bone of the wrist, and over all mark a sign like half a circle above the body; then heat the following cautery.
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it becomes white and emits no smell.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then reset the balls to their place; and have the assistants hold his hand so that it does not go back; and properly manipulate the thighs of the patient, and put a cushion under him and a strap on the thighs, and another one holding his hands; then apply the cautery at the same spot with all your strength, and keep it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat again until you come to the bone; and be careful that the ball does not jump when you are performing the cauterization; so as not to burn it; and thus cause the patient's death or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cauterization, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterization of children should be done carefully according to their size, and for adults it should be proportionate to theirs; after three days treat the area with butter ointment until the burn is healed; then apply other dressings until it is fully healed, and have the patient lie on their back for forty days so that the wound can properly heal; and make sure they are well-nourished for a long time, so that the mouth does not open when trying to get up from bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when they wish to get up, provide them with a well-made bandage and wear it for another forty days; ensure proper rest, limit their work, avoid excessive consumption of food and drink, and refrain from excessive shouting; once these instructions are followed, complete healing can be achieved.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I shall now speak of the treatment for amputation, in its own chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of abdominal rupture.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdominal regions and are known, and you see that they do not increase further, then apply the appropriate cautery as per its quantity, and burn one-third of the heart; afterwards treat it as we have said; and some ancients say that it must be cauterized with a triple-angled cautery in this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the spot with an X and draw one line across the width above the rupture, then another perpendicular to it, and hold your hand over the entire cautery instrument.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the initial cauterization is lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any limb, whether from falling or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it is necessary that the patient be cauterized with a tool called a "point," and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb, its thickness, weakness, strength, and location of twists and pains.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is successful, that's good; if not, apply another cautery over the previous one, for it is customary to move on to the nearby limb, so you must perform cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The months are aided sometimes by cauterization for great relief, especially illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	As you cannot watch the cauterization, take note if the patient is at the beginning of their illness and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, neither decreasing nor staying the same, and if you doubt that corruption may spread throughout the whole body, then make five cauterizations on the head: one in the middle of the head at nine o'clock, another towards the front at the end of the hair; and two on the two corners, with one behind on the nape; leave your hand there until the cauterization reaches the bone, and so that scabs may form to let vapors from thick humors escape; and cauterize it according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	Et si la maladie est partout dispersée ; elle perd manifestement, il faut donc que tu le cautérises avec ces cautères que nous avons dit pour la tête, et un cautère sur le nez, deux cautères sur la colonne vertébrale du cou, six cautères sur la colonne vertébrale du dos, un grand cautère sur l'omoplate et un autre à côté, deux cautères sur les épaules ; deux cautères sur les coudes, deux cautères sur les tendons de la cuisse, un cautère sur chaque joint des mains et des pieds, et sur les creux des mains ; sois prudent avec les nerfs qui sont sur le talon arrière, pour ne pas les brûler ; parfois on fait un cautère sur l'os du poignet, un autre sur l'os de l'estomac, et un autre sur le foie.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more I do cauterization, the more help I provide, and it benefits them; and know that patients feel no pain during cautery as healthy people do, because their body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	The cautery should be large and small depending on the limbs and joints, according to what you find appropriate for the tools at hand.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply flour paste with honey to the wound and use other treatments until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicine, oils, and poultices but does not heal, then make a cautery on the member according to its size; let the cautery be somewhat deep inside the bone marrow; treat it with ointments until it heals.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And sometimes cauterization is performed on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed; but nonetheless no one should attempt it unless they are knowledgeable about limbs and the paths of moving nerves.
de albaras	Of erysipelas.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the illness called 'erysipelas' persists and medicinal remedies are ineffective, then cauterize it with a perfect cauterization, according to the quantity of the heart's species, until the whiteness is removed, and its color changes; then treat it with flour made from vetch and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and pigeon blood and blackbird blood, each in equal parts; mix everything together, wrap it in a cloth, and apply it to the site until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer with cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer appears at the beginning, and you wish to stop its growth, cauterize it with a circular cautery, all around the circumference of the cancerous area.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And yet the wise ones say that a cautery should also be applied to the center of the cancer; however, I do not think this is good, as I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, which has already happened on several occasions in my experience; and it is more correct that it be cauterized around the edges, with a circular cautery, as we have mentioned before regarding various types of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	On swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has an illness called "adubelati," and it takes a long time to die, either due to the excess flesh it produces or because of the water in the patient when they are decrepit (that is, very old) and have little blood, or due to the season; and you wish to hasten their death: then cauterize them with many small cauteries all around, pricking [the skin]; afterward, leave them be.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the entire cauterization, then heat the cautery with what it is formed from:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of that illness which is called 'adubelati' until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let it be such a cautery that the patient feels it from outside in such a way that the course of decay is lessened.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards, treat until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the treatment with fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another kind of illness which is called 'corrodens', and it is nothing but a wasting away of the limbs, for it withers the limbs just as fire withers dry branches.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this illness in a place that can tolerate fire cautery together, then heat the small and large clavicle cauterizers as much as is appropriate for the location where the illness is; afterward cauterize it from all sides so that you eradicate all corruption, leaving nothing of it behind to ensure everything that was corrupted has been removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply on the cauterized areas an ointment ground up with oil so that the scaldings from the fire are removed, along with all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterward treat it with ointments producing flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days you see that healthy flesh is not forming, it's good; and if it isn't, then restart the cauterization over what remains of the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this treatment has sometimes been cured by medicine without fire cautery; however, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already described the cure with medicine in another section: use it when you need to.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	inflamed blisters that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often the feet become afflicted with a disease we call "claws," which are faulty growths that wound the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And there are two ways of cauterizing this disease.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cautery is when you heat a hollow iron rod, shaped like a quill, made of good iron to fit the claw tightly with thin edges; after heating it well, place it on the claw and turn your hand around the claw until it reaches the base; leave it there for three days until it starts to discharge pus; then apply an ointment of wild mallows crushed with honey, leaving the ointment overnight, and the claw will fall off, uprooted from its root.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the place of injury by applying ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	If they are converted by evil in the body, and happen often in hands and feet, then you must apply cauterization with hot water; it is done like this: take a copper or iron rod, or a goose quill, and place on it cloves and althelul, which means warts; put the rod over them so that it touches all around, then add a bit of hot water, hold your hand steady, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the rod reaches the root of the clove, allowing the hot water to penetrate deep down to the root; let the patient endure the scalding for an hour; leave them be like this, and it will uproot all its roots entirely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you eradicate all those that are in the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The doctor for shaking/trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When some tremble from coldness of nerves or from quartan fever or any other illness, you should apply four cauterizations or five on the spine of the back, one between each vertebra; one cautery on the foot, and one on the stomach in an olive-like shape; this will stop them shaking and hasten recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	Stinking blisters/pustules.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes the body breaks out in baths/sores or stinking blisters which come from gross corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And sometimes they cauterize it at the beginning when it appears, in this manner, and it cannot grow from there onwards, but the surplus is removed from which it comes, and they are healed; but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often there are great outpourings of blood from the artery that is severed at the wound which comes above, or the incision on the abscess, or the cauterization of the limb, and similar things; and it is very difficult to staunch.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And nonetheless when this happens to someone, hurry to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and squeeze it very hard so that the blood is stilled beneath your finger, and no more drops fall out; then take many small and large olive oil cauterizers all red-hot; then take one, either a big or little one depending on the wound and where the artery has been cut off, and place the cauterizer on that vein where you are holding your finger, and hold the cauterizer there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if there is a spark when you lift your finger above the wound, and the cauterization has ended, then take another of the hot cauteries immediately.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	Do not cease doing one after the other until the blood is staunched; and take care that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and ensure no other ill befalls the patient; and know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be well staunched especially if the artery is large, unless by one of four methods we have mentioned: cauterization, extraction if it is untreated, strong binding with thread, or medicines applied to staunch the blood; and bind it firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	What will bring about staunching is binding tightly with linen cloths or putting hot things on it, or other similar methods, and nothing else profits therefrom.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this occurs to someone and they have neither mirror nor medicine present, one must place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and fully extend it so that it is stretched above the wound and the vein; do not move the finger but moisten it with cold water often, very cold water until the blood becomes congealed, thickened and clotted; then prepare in advance what you need for cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter about all illnesses that require fire cauterization or burning medicine and their signs, causes, instruments, and types of cautery; I placed this chapter on the head down to the feet so that you can more easily find what you are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, as I begin this work, dear child, you must learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first about cauterization, and thus it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many types of people come seeking treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	They come of such a sort who are so afraid with their illness that they easily die from the shock of discovering its severity and wickedness; and of these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are some who will give you their opinion, saying: "Wait, I am healed"; but the illness is stubborn.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	You should not agree with those who come to you with such opinions, but rather put more trust in your honour than your greed, and do not act foolishly but wisely in matters that you are certain of, from which you can gain profit and recognition; and use prognoses and indications in treating your patients for their recovery, and this will help you achieve a good reputation, glory, and praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	My dear son, may our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and if he wills to inspire you with his holy breath, so be it.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have ordered this chapter for you by dividing it into chapters, according to what is presented in the previous chapter on cauterization, which I explained from head to toe so that you may find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	A head full of water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness often arises in children at birth when the midwife grips the child's head too tightly; sometimes it comes from an unknown cause as well.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this illness occur except in children, and death hastened all those whom I have treated for it; therefore, it seems best to leave such treatment of this ailment to specialists.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child whose shoulder was full of fluid, and his head swelled each day to the point where he could not support it; and the moisture grew so much that it caused death, and this moisture is gathered beneath the bone above the scapula, between the heart and the bone; and when the work is such that the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make an incision in the head as wide as two fingers; and let it be as long as a Roman mile, so that the moisture flows out; and see here the form of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see the sutures of the head opening on each side, and the fluid springs out when you press it with your hand inside, but it does not respond to your touch: then you must make three incisions in the head according to this pattern:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture quickly.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After applying compresses and powders, bind it with wine and oil, leaving it thus for five days; then unbind it, treat the wound with bandages and ointments, keep the head immobile in a similar way, and feed the patient dry meat to avoid moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is to look where the swelling and collection of pus are evident; for sometimes it is in front, sometimes behind, sometimes on the right, and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Make an incision there where the abscess is apparent and pus has accumulated, then cut it open according to your ability; take care not to sever the artery; if blood gushes out, let the patient die from loss of blood and moisture evacuation.
de reume	Of rheumatism.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and it is an old illness that does not benefit from medical treatment, then the last resort is cauterization along with cutting of the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Thus, when you are to cut the veins, have the patient bend their head back; after that, rub the place with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then hold the patient's neck tight with a cloth; then look where the vein beats, and the lines on either side are behind the ears, and they are full of blood; then mark these lines, and cut both one by one with a sharp spatule in two parts, so that the incision reaches down to the bone, and it should be across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula beneath the artery and the cup above, cutting also as II must across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, blood will continually spurt upwards forcefully.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If the artery does not open to feeling, you must measure the length of three fingers, then lacerate down to the bone; and what is required from blood to flow out is six halves, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on how much the patient can bear, and the fullness of the artery; then observe the wound: if it remains above the bone without any sign of suppuration, then extract abscesses that have formed, then reopen the wound and bind it, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes, with a thick discharge due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and an old, persistent headache with similar symptoms, and no medical treatment helps, we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have explained.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is such that the patient should pluck the hairs from their temples and look for the artery which appears in the temple, as it shows clearly by its pulse, unless it is very deep in men who are too cold-blooded; if it is deep, then the patient should constrict his neck with some cloth, then rub the place with a rough cloth and pour hot water over it until the artery appears visibly; then take the spatule whose shape is as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with pincers, and remove any tissue that is beneath each part; if the artery is delicate, turn it to the tip of the unciner, then cut off that part according to the amount of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood cannot flow out completely everywhere.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And drain the blood from the six fingers, up to three; and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread, so that gangrene does not come before the healing of the wound, and the bleeding comes accordingly; then cut off the superfluity that is between the two ligatures at the same time, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with the hot iron up to the bone until the fingers are cut; and this is a dangerous operation, if the patient does not have a fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For cauterization is helpful to dry out moisture, thus it is most useful for wet conditions.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries, one should fill the space with old cotton and place well-made bandages on top; and when they are released, ensure to treat with dry medicines that promote flesh growth, and with bandages until it is healed; and if there is bleeding from the artery while you work, quickly cut with a cauterization tool or use vitriol and squeeze the blood vessel in your hand to stop the flow; and if these are not present, put your finger on the area until the blood clots, then wash the area with cold water until the bleeding stops, and keep it compressed as required; what is important and quicker for artery extraction is that you cauterize the wound with this sharp cautery in two parts, but ensure the incisions are deep to retain heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have a space of one finger's breadth between the two blades, and then when you have hit the two places, put the hot iron on until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein into two parts; let them be separated between the two shoulders because this cautery is not continuous from end to end; and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When tears run down from the veins that are above the top of the head due to fire, and it is of no benefit to treat with medicine what one does, and you see the patient's face turn red, and feel a sensation of trembling on the forehead; and their eyes are thin and moist so that the hair of the eyelids has fallen out, and the eyelids are scalded by the heat of the tears, then it is necessary to perform this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	From the incision that is above the temple up to the second incision; remove all the scalp that is between the two incisions down to the bone, then do likewise from the middle incision up to the other second one, and then extract this spatula-shaped object.
